Rights_Init = {
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			isValidEmpty = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_city = yes
			}			
			set_key = { lhs = Tmp_8 value = 100 }
			subtract_key = { lhs = Tmp_8 which = Prov_BUPow }
			multiply_key = { lhs = Tmp_8 value = 0.004 }
			
			set_key = { lhs = Tmp_9 value = 1 }
			subtract_key = { lhs = Tmp_9 which = Tmp_8 }
			multiply_key = { lhs = Tmp_9 which = pv_ce }
			multiply_key = { lhs = Tmp_9 value = 0.01 }
			change_key = { lhs = Tmp_9 which = Tmp_8 }
			
			multiply_key = { lhs = BU_PrpResources which = Tmp_9 }
			set_key = { lhs = Tmp_8 value = 0 }
			set_key = { lhs = Tmp_9 value = 0 }
			
			multiply_key = { lhs = BU_PrpBuilding which = pv_ce }
			multiply_key = { lhs = BU_PrpBuilding value = 0.01 }
		}
		else = {
			set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpResources value = 0 }
			set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpBuilding value = 0 }
		}
	}
}



Rights_RegionInitReforms = {
	# Generic reforms
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			isValidCountry = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_reform = Pol_Structure1
					has_reform = Pol_Structure2
					has_reform = Pol_Structure3
					has_reform = Pol_Structure4
					has_reform = Pol_Structure5
				}
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp0 which = Pol_Structure }
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp1 value = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #### dont save until the setup is properly adjusted
				always = no
				OR = {
					has_reform = Pol_Centralisation1
					has_reform = Pol_Centralisation2
					has_reform = Pol_Centralisation3
					has_reform = Pol_Centralisation4
					has_reform = Pol_Centralisation5
				}
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp2 which = Pol_Centralisation }
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp3 value = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_reform = Pol_Autonomy1
					has_reform = Pol_Autonomy2
				}
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp4 which = Pol_Autonomy }
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp5 value = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_reform = Pol_Provincial1
					has_reform = Pol_Provincial2
					has_reform = Pol_Provincial3
				}
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp6 which = Pol_Provincial }
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp7 value = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_reform = Pol_Military1
					has_reform = Pol_Military2
					has_reform = Pol_Military3
					has_reform = Pol_Military4
				}
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp8 which = Pol_Military }
			set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp9 value = 1 }
		}
		add_government_reform = Pol_Structure2
		add_government_reform = Pol_Centralisation2
		add_government_reform = Pol_Autonomy1
		add_government_reform = Pol_Provincial1
		add_government_reform = Pol_Military1
	}

	every_country = {
		limit = {
			isValidCountry = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp1 value = 1 }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Pol_Structure which = Tax_Tmp0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp3 value = 1 }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Pol_Centralisation which = Tax_Tmp2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp5 value = 1 }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Pol_Autonomy which = Tax_Tmp4 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp7 value = 1 }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Pol_Provincial which = Tax_Tmp6 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp9 value = 1 }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Pol_Military which = Tax_Tmp8 }
		}
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp0 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp1 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp2 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp3 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp4 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp5 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp6 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp7 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp8 value = 0 }
		set_key = { lhs = Tax_Tmp9 value = 0 }
		Pol_CentralisationUpdate = yes
	}
}
Rights_Presim = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			isValidCountry = yes
		}
		Pol_FamilyInit = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_reform = Pol_NominalEmpire } 	#key = 10
						NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire } 	#key = 3
						NOT = { has_reform = shogunate } 			#key = 4
						NOT = { has_reform = Horde_Monarchy } 		#key = 8
						NOT = { has_reform = Horde_MonarchyS }		#key = 8
						NOT = { has_reform = Yuan_Monarchy }		#key = 9
						NOT = { has_reform = free_city } 			#key = 11
						NOT = { has_reform = trading_city }			#key = 2
						NOT = { has_reform = colonial_government }	#key = 6	
					}
					is_key_equal = { lhs = Pol_Privileges value = 1 }
				}
			}
			add_government_reform = Pol_Privileges1
		}
	}
}

	greece_region = {
		set_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 70 }
		set_key = { lhs = SF_Freedom value = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = orthodox
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = albanian
				}
				set_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 35 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							primary_culture = greek
							primary_culture = osmanli
							primary_culture = pontic
						}
					}
				}
				set_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 75 }
			}
			else = {
				set_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 50 }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = SF_PrpResources value = 0.10 }
			set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpResources value = 0.45 }
			set_key = { lhs = BG_PrpResources value = 0.05 }
			set_key = { lhs = CL_PrpResources value = 0.20 }
			set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpResources value = 0.20 }

			set_key = { lhs = RE_PrpBuilding value = 0.30 }
			set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpBuilding value = 0.10 }
			set_key = { lhs = BG_PrpBuilding value = 0.30 }
			set_key = { lhs = CL_PrpBuilding value = 0.20 }
			set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpBuilding value = 0.10 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = GEN
							tag = VEN
						}
					}
				}
				set_key = { lhs = SF_PrpResources value = 0.25 }
				set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpResources value = 0.30 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = EPI
							tag = MOE
						}
					}
				}
				set_key = { lhs = SF_PrpResources value = 0.25 }
				set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpResources value = 0.30 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 35 }
			set_key = { lhs = SF_PrpResources value = 0.10 }
			set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpResources value = 0.50 }
			set_key = { lhs = BG_PrpResources value = 0.05 }
			set_key = { lhs = CL_PrpResources value = 0.20 }
			set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpResources value = 0.15 }

			set_key = { lhs = RE_PrpBuilding value = 0.25 }
			set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpBuilding value = 0.10 }
			set_key = { lhs = BG_PrpBuilding value = 0.45 }
			set_key = { lhs = CL_PrpBuilding value = 0.15 }
			set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpBuilding value = 0.05 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = GEN
							tag = VEN
						}
					}
				}
				set_key = { lhs = SF_PrpResources value = 0.30 }
				set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpResources value = 0.30 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
			}
			#Tax_EnableProperty = yes
			#Tax_EnableToll = yes
			#Tax_EnableInheritance = yes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						owner = { tag = BYZ }
					}
				}
				#Tax_EnableStateServiceRequirement = yes
			}
			else = {
				#Tax_EnableServiceVolunteer = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			#Tax_EnableStateServiceDues = yes
			#Tax_EnableServiceVolunteer = yes
		}
	}

					NOT = { is_nomad = yes }
				}
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_TRPow value = 30 } }
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 25 }
		}
		else = {
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 5 }
		}
		set_key = { lhs = SF_Freedom value = 40 }
		set_key = { lhs = SF_PrpResources value = 0.15 }
		set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpResources value = 0.35 }
		set_key = { lhs = BG_PrpResources value = 0.05 }
		set_key = { lhs = CL_PrpResources value = 0.30 }
		set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpResources value = 0.15 }

		set_key = { lhs = RE_PrpBuilding value = 0.30 }
		set_key = { lhs = NO_PrpBuilding value = 0.10 }
		set_key = { lhs = BG_PrpBuilding value = 0.45 }
		set_key = { lhs = CL_PrpBuilding value = 0.20 }
		set_key = { lhs = BU_PrpBuilding value = 0.05 }
		#Tax_EnableLand = yes
		#Tax_EnableStateServiceDues = yes
		set_province_flag = Infra_Capitol100

		#set_province_flag = Infra_Amenities25
